The hotel is located on the bank of Tianmu Lake, surrounded by lush bamboo forests, and the scenery is very beautiful. Every morning I wake up and enjoy the serene natural view from the window of my room, which makes me feel very comfortable and peaceful.

The hotel rooms are very spacious, clean and comfortable. The furniture and decoration in the room are very elegant and give people a warm feeling. The bed was very comfortable and I was able to get a good sleep every night. In addition, the room also provides modern facilities, such as air conditioning, TV, mini refrigerator, etc., which made my stay very convenient.

The service at the hotel is also excellent. The staff was always friendly, welcoming, and always ready to answer my questions and help. Their professional attitude and attentive service made me feel welcome. The hotel also provides a wealth of facilities and services, such as a gym, swimming pool and spa, allowing me to relax and unwind.

I was also impressed with the hotel's dining options. Their restaurant offers a variety of cuisine options, including local specialties and international cuisine. I tried their breakfast buffet, which was varied, fresh and delicious. Whether it's Chinese pastries or Western omelettes, they can satisfy the needs of different tastes. At dinner, I also tasted their special dishes, which were delicious and unforgettable.

Bamboo Valley Hotel is also an ideal choice for those who enjoy nature and outdoor activities. There are many hiking and trekking routes around the hotel, allowing you to explore the surrounding natural scenery. In addition, the hotel also provides bicycle rental services for guests to explore the surrounding areas.

Overall, I was very satisfied with my stay at Bamboo Valley Hotel. The hotel's beautiful environment, comfortable rooms, and excellent service from the butler (Huang Xinlai) made me have a pleasant and unforgettable vacation. If you are planning a trip to the Tianmu Lake area, I highly recommend Bamboo Valley Hotel as your accommodation choice.

msg:Changzhou, the first stop of the summer vacation, chose the No. 1 place in the local hotel list, and the overall feeling is still good!
[Location] Located in Xinbei District of Changzhou, it is considered a new district. It is near the municipal government and various government agencies, as well as Changzhou Museum, Library and Art Museum. It is adjacent to the Civic Square. It's also very convenient to take a taxi. There is a subway station nearby within a three-minute walk. I would like to give a big thumbs up to the locationüëç

[Environment] Walking into the hotel lobby feels bright and cool. The hotel is not small, with a restaurant and gym, and a small coffee shop on the first floor. The cakes are delicious!

[Room] We booked a deluxe twin room, but the two single beds can be pushed together. My daughter and I sleep on this big bed, which is very comfortable and the mattress is very soft. The size of the room is not too small, and the size of the bathroom and toilet is also spacious. I am very satisfied with the room!

[Service] The service is good. Just after entering the hotel, there is a waiter pushing the luggage. The service at the front desk is very enthusiastic with a smile.

[Food] We didn't have breakfast in the hotel so we won't comment, but the room provides plenty of mineral water every day, as well as drinks and snacks. In the evening, there are fruits and yogurt. The quality is good and it is very considerate.

In short, the hotel is still very satisfactory overall, but let me ask three questions: 1. The sound insulation of the room is very poor, and the sound of snoring in the next room can be heard clearly. 2. There is a strong durian smell in the refrigerator. It is estimated that the last guest put durian food in the refrigerator. The smell was still there when we checked out after staying for three nights! 3. The hair dryer is too difficult to use. If you want to dry long hair, it takes half an hour, and the noise is loud...
I hope the hotel can find a way to solve the above problems. If we go to Changzhou again, we will still consider staying here. I recommend it to everyone!
